-04- COMMANDS
------------------------------------------------------------

Dispel
-------
Use the skill 'Dispel'

FireLif
-------
Use the combo Fire 3 + LifeShaver.

L3Muddl
-------
Use the skill 'L.3 Muddle'

LulSlow
-------
Use the combo Lullaby + Slow.

Lullaby
-------
Use the skill 'Lullaby'

R-Bolt
-------
Use a random lightning-elemental skill.

  (2/16 chance each)  Bolt Beam, Bolt Edge, Diffuser, Plasma
  (1/16 chance each)  Bolt, Bolt 2, Bolt 3, Giga Volt, Mega Volt, Ramuh, Tek Laser, WaveCannon

R-Heavy
-------
Use a random percentage-damage skill.

  (2/16 chance each)  Cave In, Launcher, Missile
  (1/16 chance each)  Cyclonic, Demi, Grav Bomb, Lode Stone, Quartr, Shimsham, Slash, Snowball, Sonic Boom, W Wind

R-Level
-------
Use a random level-based skill.

  (5/8 chance each)  L.5 Doom
  (1/8 chance each)  L.3 Muddle, L.4 Flare, L.? Pearl

SafAcid
-------
Use the combo Safe + Acid Rain.

UniBolt
-------
Use the combo Unicorn + Bolt Beam.

------------------------------------------------------------

2. down, up, down, down-right, right
3. R, left, up-left, up
4. Y, L, down, down-right, right, left
5. X, right, down-right, down, down-left, left
6. up, up-right, right, left, X, L
7. left, left, right, down-right, down, down-left, left
8. Y, L, X, L, X, right, up-right, up, down
